DGUNG LO BZHI LNGA'I THOG NAS YI GE 'BRI KLOG DANG SUM RTAGS
SOGS LA THUGS GZHOL, DGUNG LO BRGYAD KYI THOG RGYAL DBANG LNGA
PA'I SKU MDUN DU BCAR NAS MDO SNGAGS SOGS SPYI DANG BYE BRAG GI
GZHUNG DON MANG PO GSAN, 'DAR PA LO TZ'A LAS SKAR RTZIS DANG,

MKHAS GRUB GNYIS LDAN GYI YONGS 'DZIN DU MA BSTEN NAS THUN MIN
DANG THUN MONG GI RIG GNAS KUN LA DPYIS PHYIN PAR MDZAD, RGYAL
DBANG LNGA PA CHEN POS CHOS SRID GNYIS KA'I RGYAL TSAB KYI LAS
KA BSTZAL BAS LO NYI SHU RTZA DRUG GI RING SDE SRID BZUNG NAS
SRID BSKYANGS, RTZE PHO BRANG DMAR PO NYAMS GSO DANG RGYA SKYED
GNANG, RGYAL DBANG LNGA PA'I GSER GDUNG 'DZAM GLING RGYAN GCIG
BZHENGS, GSO BA RIG PA'I DPAL LDAN RGYUD BZHI LA ZHUS DAG MDZAD
DE DPAR DU BSKRUN PA SOGS MDZAD RJES SHIN TU CHE, GSUNG RTZOM
SKOR LA PHUG LUGS RTZIS KYI LEGS BSHAD BEEd'URYA DKAR PO DANG,
BEEd'URYA DKAR PO'I GA-YA' SEL, GSER GDUNG 'DZAM GLING RGYAN
GCIG GI DKAR CHAG KHRIMS YIG DVANGS SHEL NYER GCIG  GSO BA RIG
PA'I KHOG 'BUBS LEGS BSHAD BEEd'URYA'I ME LONG DRANG SRONG DGYES
PA'I DGA' STON, DPAL LDAN RGYUD BZHI'I 'GREL PA BEEd'URYA SNGON
MO, MAN NGAG RGYUD KYI LHAN THABS DUS MIN 'CHI ZHAGS GCOD PA'I
RAL GRI SOGS LEGS BSHAD RMAD DU BYUNG BA'I BSTAN BCOS SNA TSOGS
POD NYI SHU RTZA DRUG TZAM MDZAD, GSO BA RIG PA'I DPAL LDAN

GRANGS MED PA BLUGS NAS, LCAGS BSREGS KYI THO BA RI RAB TZAM PA

DANG, RI THAMS CAD RA LUG LA SOGS PA'I MGO BRNYAN CAN GYI RVA
RTZE ME 'BAR BAS RDUNG KHA BKYE BA'I BAR DU DMYAL BA'I SEMS CAN
